Each song or call is annotated with what it means such as alarm, territorial, attraction, etc.\r\n\r\n▶ CONFORMS TO ABA AND AOU STANDARDS –iBird follows standards set by the American Ornithological Union and the American Birding Association. As an example iBird correctly splits of the Winter Wren into the Winter and Pacific types. \r\n\r\n▶ FIRST NAME, LAST NAME OR TAXONOMIC SORT – Sort species in taxonomic (evolutionary) as well as alphabetic order.\r\n\r\nAWARDS and ACCOLADES for iBird:\r\n\r\niBird has won more awards for excellence than any birding app on the market.
